I don't get how my house can be falling apart so quickly. When we were buying and picking our materials it was fine but once as we started to talk about the lay out it was so complicated and then this guy named Brandon didn't do the carpet right. He did the carpet horizontal and it just looks weird. The only person that was helpful was Maryanne.
She is a great person to work with when you are buying the house because she helps you.
The place itself is very clean and calm. But I suggest when you are buying to take pictures of the models they show you and how you want it built and done. <text>I appreciate the steps they're taking for COVID safety, which factor into the wait time. I saw a lot of facility cleaning going on. They were efficient, friendly, and professional. No complaints. I got an exam, a cleaning, and 4 fillings done in the span of a week, but I got lucky and swooped in on a cancellation. They're pretty busy.

Mayra was very sweet at the reception desk and helped put me at ease. As a person in customer service, I know how much energy that takes to maintain all day and I appreciated it very much. The doctor who gave me the fillings was a man of few words but he was kind and checked in with me often to make sure I was comfortable.

This  place is definitely no frills/low budget. The lobby isn't particularly inviting aesthetically, and I was nervous after reading some less than stellar reviews. With insurance, it seems that you either pay with more time (wait time) or you pay with more money (pricier insurance). At around $8 a month for my dental insurance, I fully expect to pay with more time and am OK with that.

Across 3 appointments, my best wait time was a speedy 10 minutes (last appointment of the day.) The worst wait was 90 minutes, which didn't bother me as I had read reviews about long waits and was prepared for it with nothing else planned afterward. The other wait was around 40 minutes. I used the time to clean out my car, but you could also just bring a book or go somewhere close by to pass the time until you get the text that they're ready for you.

Ignore the lesser reviews and give them a chance, I'm pleasantly surprised at the service I got.<//text>< user>
